Praise the room service. There are always 4 bottles of water in the room. If they say there is not enough soap, they will directly put 3 pieces. It's a surprise and a thumbs up.

After 18:00, the dessert cakes in the lobby bar are half price, you can try your luck.

Breakfast is good until 10 o'clock.

The swimming pool environment is good, you can steam sauna without being afraid of cold air, and the best thing is that it opens at 6 o'clock in the morning.

The abstract red ornaments at the end of the weird long corridor.
